<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>IT
Tech Packaging, Inc. Announces Fourth Quarter and Fiscal Year 2021 Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Company
to Host Earnings Conference Call on Tuesday, March 15, 2022, at 8:30 am ET</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;March
15, 2022&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ --&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the fourth&nbsp;quarter&nbsp;and audited financial results for the fiscal year&nbsp;ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Mr.
Zhenyong Liu, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented, &ldquo;We are pleased with our performance for the fiscal
year 2021, as we demonstrated excellent revenue growth and improved business efficiencies. In fiscal year 2021, our business execution
was reflected as we reached approximately $160.88 million in revenue with an increase of59% year-over-year and approximately $11.02 millionin
gross profit with an increase of 93% year-over-year. In fiscal year 2021, we launched a series of initiatives to optimize our revenue
structure and diversify our business, which led to a very encouraging results. We significantly improved our operating and cost efficiency,reducing
our sell, general and administrative expense by 14.3%, while maintaining the solid growth of overall sales volume and average selling
prices of CMP products and offset printing paper products. Looking forward, with our dedicated effort and commitment, we believe our
business fundamentals will continue to support our leading position in the industry and growin the foreseeable future.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Fourth
Quarter 2021 Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="padding-bottom: 1.5pt; font-weight: bold"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

 Ended&nbsp;December 31,</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="padding-bottom: 1.5pt; font-weight: bold"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="font-style: italic"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">($

    <TD COLSPAN="2" STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; text-align: center; font-weight: bold"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">2020</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1.5pt; font-weight: bold"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1.5pt; font-weight: bold"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom; background-color: rgb(204,238,255)">
    <TD STYLE="width: 64%"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenues</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 9%; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">45.05</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 9%; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">32.48</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 9%; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">38.7</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">%</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">For
the fourth quarter of 2021, total revenue increased by&nbsp;approximately $12.6 million, or 38.7%, to&nbsp;approximately $45.0 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$32.5 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The increase in total revenue was mainly due to the increase in sales volume of
CMP.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from CMP, including both regular CMP and light-Weight CMP, increased by&nbsp;$14.7 million, or 59.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $39.7 million&nbsp;and
accounted for 88.0% of total revenue for the fourth quarter of 2021, compared to&nbsp;approximately $24.9 million, or 76.7% of total
revenue, for the same period of last year. The Company sold 69,953tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$567/tonne in the fourth quarter of
2021, compared to 57,627tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$432/tonne in the same period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Of
the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP increased by&nbsp;approximately $13.0million, or 66.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $32.7 million,
resulting from sales of 57,410tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$569/tonne, during the fourth quarter of 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately
$19.7 million, resulting from sales of 45,210 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$435/tonne, for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight
CMP increased by&nbsp;approximately $1.8 million, or 33.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $7.0 million, resulting from sales of 12,543tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$558/tonne for the fourth quarter of 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $5.2 million, resulting from sales
of 12,417 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$422/tonne for the same period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

at an ASP of&nbsp;$994/tonne, for the fourth quarter of 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $2.6million, resulting from sales
of 3,165tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$837/tonne for the same period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

from face masks increased by&nbsp;$110,993, or 314.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $146,282&nbsp;&nbsp;for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021, from $35,289 for the same period of 2020. The Company sold 3,014 thousand pieces of face masks for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021, compared to 445 thousand pieces of face masks for the same period of 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Gross
Profit and Gross Margin</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
cost of sales increased by&nbsp;$9.0 million, or 28.3%, to&nbsp;approximately $40.7 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2021 from&nbsp;approximately
$31.7 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. For paper products, overall cost of sales per tonne was&nbsp;$533&nbsp;for the fourth
quarter of 2021, compared to&nbsp;$462&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The increase in overall cost of sales was mainly due to
the increased manufacturing overhead costs and increased material costs, specifically higher average unit purchase costs of recycled
paper board and recycled white scrap paper in the fourth quarter of 2021.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight
CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$514,&nbsp;$490,&nbsp;$596 and&nbsp;$1,132, respectively, for the fourth
quarter of 2021, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;$429,&nbsp;$406,&nbsp;$534, and&nbsp;$962, respectively, for the same period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $4.3million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2021, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately

quarter of 2021, compared to 2.3% for the same period of last year. Gross profit (loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset
printing paper, tissue paper products and face mask products were 9.6%, 12.2%, 21.5%, -13.9% and 25.2%, respectively, for the fourth

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

the fourth quarter of 2021 from&nbsp;approximately $2.7 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>EBITDA</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">EBITDA
was&nbsp;approximately $8.7 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2021, compared to&nbsp;approximately $2.6 million&nbsp;for the same
period of last year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Note
1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">In
addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the
Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation
and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes
this measure is useful to investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations,
the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed
as an alternative to measures of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Reconciliation
of Net Income to EBITDA</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>(Amounts
expressed in US$)</B></FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 6; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->6<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P><P STYLE="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Revenue</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">For
the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, total revenue increased by&nbsp;$59.9 million, or 59.4%, to&nbsp;approximately $160.9 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$100.9 million&nbsp;for 2020. The increase in total revenue was mainly due to an increase in sales volume of CMP and offset printing
paper and increase in ASPs of CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products, partially offset by the decrease in sales volume
of tissue paper products.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
following table summarizes revenue, volume and ASP by product for the years ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;and 2020, respectively:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from CMP, including both regular CMP and light-Weight CMP increased by&nbsp;$55.4 million, or69.9%, to&nbsp;approximately $134.5 million,
and accounted for 83.6% of total revenue for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately $79.2 million,
or 78.4% of total revenue for 2020. The Company sold 259,691tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$518/tonne in the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021, compared to 196,885tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$402/tonne in 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Of
the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP increased by&nbsp;$48.8 million, or 78.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $111.1 million, resulting
from sales of 213,490tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$520/tonne during the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately
$62.3 million, resulting from sales of 154,084tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$404/tonne for 2020. Revenue from light-weight CMP increased by&nbsp;$6.6
million, or 39.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $23.4million, resulting from sales of 46,201tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$507/tonne for the year
ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $16.8million, resulting from sales of 42,801tonnes at an ASP
of&nbsp;$393/tonne for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->7<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P><P STYLE="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"></P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from offset printing paper increased by&nbsp;$4.8 million, or 39.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $17.1 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $12.3 million&nbsp;for 2020. The Company sold 24,513tonnes of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$696/tonne
in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to 20,358tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$603/tonne in 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from tissue paper products increased by&nbsp;$0.4 million, or 4.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $8.8 million, resulting from sales of 8,255tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,062/tonne, for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $8.4 million, resulting
from sales of 10,088tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$834/tonne for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from face masks decreased by&nbsp;$0.6 million, or 51.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.5 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31,
2021, from approximately $1.1 million for 2020. The Company sold 12,664 thousand pieces of face masks for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021, compared to 10,301 thousand pieces of face masks for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Gross
Profit and Gross Margin</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
cost of sales increased by $54.6 million, or 57.4%, to&nbsp;approximately $149.9 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$95.2 million&nbsp;for 2020. The increase in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the increased sales volume of CMP and offset printing
paper and increased material costs in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight
CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products were,&nbsp;$487,&nbsp;$463,&nbsp;$570, and&nbsp;$1,214, respectively, for the year
ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;compared to&nbsp;$383,&nbsp;$358,&nbsp;$498, and&nbsp;$1,015, respectively, for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
gross profit increased by&nbsp;$5.3million, or 93.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $11.0million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$5.7 million&nbsp;for 2020. Overall gross margin increased by 1.2percentage points to 6.9% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;from
5.7% for 2020. Gross margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products and face mask products were
6.3%, 8.7%, 18.2%, -14.3% and 19.2%, respectively, for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to 5.4%, 8.9%, 17.3%, -21.7% and
48.1%, respectively, for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Selling,
General and Administrative Expenses</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">SG&amp;A
expenses decreased by&nbsp;$1.6 million, or 14.3%, to&nbsp;approximately $9.6 million&nbsp;for the yearended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$11.2 million&nbsp;for 2020. As a percentage of total revenue, SG&amp;A expenses was 5.9% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021,
compared to 11.1% for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Income
(Loss) from Operations</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Income
from operations increased by&nbsp;$6.9 million, or 126.8% to&nbsp;approximately $1.5 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31,
2021&nbsp;from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately $5.5 million&nbsp;for 2020. Operating margin was 0.9% for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2021, compared to operating loss margin of 5.4% for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Net
Income (Loss)</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Net
Income increased by&nbsp;$6.5  million, or 116.3%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.9 million, or earnings per basic and diluted share of&nbsp;$0.02,
for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $5.6 million, or loss per basic and diluted share
of&nbsp;$0.21 for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">EBITDA
increased by&nbsp;$12.7million, or 125.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $22.9 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2021&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$10.2 million&nbsp;for 2020.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Note
1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">In
addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the
Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation
and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes
this measure is useful to investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations,
the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed
as an alternative to measures of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

playback will be available through&nbsp;11:00 am ET&nbsp;on&nbsp;March 15, 2022&nbsp;to&nbsp;8:59 am ET&nbsp;on&nbsp;March 23, 2022.
To listen, please dial+1-855-452-5696 if calling from the&nbsp;United States, or +61-281-990-299 if calling internationally. Use the
conference ID 4898872 to access the replay.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
IT Tech Packaging, Inc.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Founded
in 1996, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North
China. Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes
three categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based
in Baoding and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>
